[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Comprehensive Fix Strategy for Type1Lexer OOM Vulnerability[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m. Root Cause Analysis[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe OOM error occurs in `[0m[1;35mType1Lexer.readCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` at line [0m[1;36m507[0m[39m, where a byte [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39marray is allocated based on an untrusted integer value from PDF font data without [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39many validation:[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbyte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m data = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlength[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Line [0m[1;36m507[0m[39m - Unbounded allocation[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe vulnerability chain:[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. PDF contains Type1 font with malicious CharString length value [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnear [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mInteger.MAX_VALUE[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Type1Parser reads this as an INTEGER token[0m                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mType1Lexer.readToken[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m detects [0m[32m"RD"[0m[39m or [0m[32m"-|"[0m[39m token and calls [0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mprevToken.intValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. [0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m attempts to allocate a massive byte array, exceeding JVM limits[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. OutOfMemoryError occurs, triggering FuzzerSecurityIssueLow[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m. Fix Strategy[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Primary Fix Location:** [0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Lexer.java`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Add Maximum CharString Length Constant[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAdd a constant after the LOG declaration [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m50[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to define a reasonable [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mupper bound for CharString sizes:[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/[0m[39m**[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * Maximum length for a single CharString. CharStrings contain encrypted glyph[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * outlines and should typically be at most a few kilobytes. This limit of 10MB[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * is chosen to be consistent with PfbParser.MAX_LENGTH patterns while preventing[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m * denial of service attacks from malicious fonts.[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate static final int MAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH = 10_000_000; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m [0m[1;36m10[0m[39m MB[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Rationale for 10MB limit:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with PfbParser's MAX_LENGTH approach [0m[1;39m([0m[39m100MB for entire font[0m[1;39m)[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Individual CharStrings [0m[1;39m([0m[39mglyph definitions[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m are typically a few hundred bytes[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Complex glyphs might reach a few kilobytes[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- 10MB provides substantial headroom while preventing OOM attacks[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Aligns with existing patterns in the codebase [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee ScratchFile, [0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRandomAccessReadMemoryMappedFile[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m#### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Add Comprehensive Validation to [0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify the `[0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m502[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m515[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to add validation [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBEFORE allocation:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Validation Order:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Check for negative length [0m[1;39m([0m[39mcorruption indicator[0m[1;39m)[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Check against MAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH [0m[1;39m([0m[39mDoS prevention[0m[1;39m)[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Check remaining buffer capacity [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpremature EOF prevention[0m[1;39m)[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. Only then perform allocation[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Implementation Pattern:**[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mFollow the validation pattern used in `[0m[1;35mDataInputByteArray.readBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m143[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m150[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which is the gold standard in the codebase:[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprivate Token [0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[39mint length[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m throws IOException[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validation [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Check for negative length[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength < [0m[1;36m0[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mDamagedFontException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Invalid negative CharString length: "[0m[39m + [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mlength [0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                      + [0m[32m" at buffer position "[0m[39m + [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mbuffer.position[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validation [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Check against maximum allowed size[0m                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength > MAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH[0m[1;39m)[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mDamagedFontException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"CharString length "[0m[39m + length [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                      + [0m[32m" exceeds maximum allowed length "[0m[39m + [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mMAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH [0m                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                                      + [0m[32m" at buffer position "[0m[39m + [0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mbuffer.position[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Validation [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Check buffer has sufficient remaining data[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Need length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m for the space separator[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    if [0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mbuffer.remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m < length + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Insufficient data in buffer for CharString of length[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [32m"[0m[39m [0m                                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                            + length + [0m[32m". Required: "[0m[39m + [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlength + [0m[1;36m1[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m                            + [0m[32m", available: "[0m[39m + [0m[1;35mbuffer.remaining[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    try[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mbuffer.get[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m; [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m space[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[1;39m][0m[39m data = new byte[0m[1;39m[[0m[39mlength[0m[1;39m][0m[39m;  [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Now safe to allocate[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[1;35mbuffer.get[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        return new [0m[1;35mToken[0m[1;39m([0m[39mdata, Token.CHARSTRING[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    catch [0m[1;39m([0m[39mBufferUnderflowException exception[0m[1;39m)[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m This should not occur due to validation above, but kept for defense in [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdepth[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m        throw new [0m[1;35mIOException[0m[1;39m([0m[32m"Premature end of buffer reached"[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Exception Choice Rationale:**[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use `DamagedFontException` for length validation failures [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines for negative and[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39moversized[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- This is consistent with existing Type1Lexer error handling [0m[1;39m([0m[39msee lines [0m[1;36m164[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m224[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Use `IOException` for buffer capacity issues [0m[1;39m([0m[39mexisting pattern at line [0m[1;36m513[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m. Why This Fix is Optimal[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Addresses the Security Issue:**[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Prevents allocation of arrays exceeding reasonable bounds[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validates untrusted input before use[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Converts potential OOM crash into graceful error handling[0m                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Preserves Existing Logic:**[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to tokenization flow[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to calling code [0m[1;39m([0m[39mType1Parser[0m[1;39m)[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- No changes to Type1Font API[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All existing tests will continue to pass [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtest uses [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte CharString[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Follows Codebase Patterns:**[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with PfbParser.MAX_LENGTH pattern [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m71[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m162[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m164[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with [0m[1;35mDataInputByteArray.readBytes[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m143[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m150[0m[1;39m)[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with [0m[1;35mCFFParser.readOffSize[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m validation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m264[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m267[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with existing DamagedFontException usage in Type1Lexer[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Defense in Depth:**[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Multiple validation layers [0m[1;39m([0m[39mnegative, max size, buffer capacity[0m[1;39m)[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Validation occurs before allocation [0m[1;39m([0m[39mprevents OOM[0m[1;39m)[0m                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Descriptive error messages aid debugging and security analysis[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Buffer capacity check prevents BufferUnderflowException[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Side Effects:**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not modify harness code or fuzzing logic[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not modify test code[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not modify external libraries[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not affect legitimate font processing[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not change API contracts[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m. Implementation Details[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**File to Modify:** [0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`fontbox/src/main/java/org/apache/fontbox/type1/Type1Lexer.java`[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Lines to Modify:**[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- After line [0m[1;36m50[0m[39m: Add MAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH constant[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Lines [0m[1;36m502[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m515[0m[39m: Replace [0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m implementation with validated version[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**No Other Files Need Modification:**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Type1Parser continues to work unchanged[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Type1Font API unchanged[0m                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Token class unchanged[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- All callers continue to work unchanged[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m5[0m[39m. Potential Edge Cases Handled[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Negative lengths**: Caught by first validation, throws DamagedFontException[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Zero length**: Passes validation, creates empty byte array [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlegitimate case[0m[1;39m)[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Normal lengths [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m1000[0m[39m bytes[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Pass all validations, work normally[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Large but valid lengths [0m[1;39m([0m[39m1KB-10MB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Pass validation, allocate successfully[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Malicious lengths [0m[1;39m([0m[39m>10MB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**: Caught by MAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH check[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Integer.MAX_VALUE**: Caught by MAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH check[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Buffer exhaustion**: Caught by [0m[1;35mremaining[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m check before allocation[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Testing Considerations[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix will:[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Pass existing tests**: The test case [0m[32m"3 RD 123"[0m[39m uses [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m-byte CharString [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwell [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39munder limit[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Fail fuzzer's malicious input**: Large length values will throw [0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mDamagedFontException[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Prevent OOM**: Array allocation only occurs after validation passes[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Provide clear diagnostics**: Error messages include length value and buffer [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mposition[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m7[0m[39m. Alternative Approaches Considered and Rejected[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Fix in Type1Parser**[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: Would require validating all INTEGER tokens, too broad[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Would not catch edge cases where lengths come from other sources[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Violates principle of validating at point of use[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Fix in [0m[1;35mToken.intValue[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: Token is a general-purpose class used throughout Type1 parsing[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Would break legitimate uses of large integers in font metadata[0m                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Too far from the actual risk point[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Catch OutOfMemoryError**[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: OOM should never occur, indicates programming error[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Catching OOM is unreliable and poor practice[0m                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Does not prevent the resource exhaustion attempt[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Alternative [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m: Use smaller limit [0m[1;39m([0m[39me.g., 1MB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m**[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Considered**: Could use 1MB instead of 10MB[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- **Rejected**: 10MB provides better compatibility with future formats[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Still prevents OOM attacks effectively[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Consistent with codebase patterns [0m[1;39m([0m[39mPfbParser uses 100MB for entire font[0m[1;39m)[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m8[0m[39m. Summary[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis fix strategy:[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Adds MAX_CHARSTRING_LENGTH constant** [0m[1;39m([0m[39m10MB[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m following PfbParser pattern[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Adds three-layer validation** in [0m[1;35mreadCharString[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m before allocation:[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Negative check → DamagedFontException[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Maximum size check → DamagedFontException  [0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Buffer capacity check → IOException[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Uses existing exception types** consistently with codebase patterns[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Provides descriptive error messages** with values and positions[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Prevents OOM** by validating before allocation[0m                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m6[0m[39m. **Preserves all existing functionality** and API contracts[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m7[0m[39m. **Requires modification of only one file** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mType1Lexer.java[0m[1;39m)[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m8[0m[39m. **Follows established validation patterns** from DataInputByteArray and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mCFFParser[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThis is a minimal, focused fix that addresses the security vulnerability at its [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mroot cause while maintaining consistency with the broader codebase architecture.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
